SENTIENT SPECIES:
Four-Armed Red Robots: Purely mechanical lifeforms, artificially created. They have red skin. They have four arms. They have bilateral symmetry. They are violent and always willing to listen. They were created by the Republic of Koboldoids and Antoids on Fynou III as servants in 1130.
	Their Stats are: STR: 0 DEX: 0 CON: 1 INT: 2 CHA: -3
Yellow Antoids: Small, industrious and well-organised, these creatures' greatest weakness is their ever-ballooning population. They have yellow skin. They have bilateral symmetry. They are cautious and deeply religious. They first evolved on Metatron IV in 968.
	Their Stats are: STR: -1 DEX: -2 CON: -1 INT: 2 CHA: 1
Scaly Humanoids with Five-fold Symmetry: Pretty adventurous but otherwise fairly average. They have five-fold symmetry. They are violent and have a deep need to conform. They first evolved on Autorog V in 1167.
	Their Stats are: STR: -1 DEX: 0 CON: 0 INT: 0 CHA: 1
White Dwarfoids: Fond of drink and industry - especially building strange contraptions. They have white skin. They have bilateral symmetry. They are violent and deeply rationalist. They first evolved on Bylox II in 1167.
	Their Stats are: STR: 1 DEX: 1 CON: 2 INT: 1 CHA: -2

CIVILISATIONS:
THE REPUBLIC OF HUMANOIDS, CATOIDS, ROBOTS, ANTOIDS AND TROLLOIDS:
An ancient, corrupt, fantastically wealthy, advanced Republic of 19 planets, with 174 billion inhabitants.
Major populations:
4 billion Four-Armed Red Robots.
152 billion Yellow Antoids.
2 billion Scaly Humanoids with Five-fold Symmetry.
16 billion enslaved White Dwarfoids.
It controls a Living Weapon.
It controls a Universal Nutrient.
It controls a Universal Computer Virus.

	Their Stats are: STR: 2 DEX: 3 CON: 3 INT: 1 CHA: 3
